height: 230px;" /></a></p> <p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size:9px;">Also known as Altarf or Tarf,<sup id="cite_ref-IAU-LSN_8-0"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-IAU-LSN-8">[7]</a></sup>&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Beta_Cancri" title="Beta Cancri">Beta Cancri</a>&nbsp;is the brightest star in Cancer at&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Apparent_magnitude" title="Apparent magnitude">apparent magnitude</a>&nbsp;3.5.<sup id="cite_ref-kalerbeta_9-0"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-kalerbeta-9">[8]</a></sup>&nbsp;Located 290 &plusmn; 30&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Light-year" title="Light-year">light-years</a>&nbsp;from Earth,<sup id="cite_ref-vanLeeuwen2007_10-0"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-vanLeeuwen2007-10">[9]</a></sup>&nbsp;it is a&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Binary_star" title="Binary star">binary star</a>&nbsp;system, its main component an&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Orange_giant" title="Orange giant">orange giant</a>&nbsp;of spectral type K4III that is varies slightly from a baseline magnitude of 3.53&mdash;dipping by 0.005 magnitude over a period of 6 days.<sup id="cite_ref-AAVSObeta_11-0"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-AAVSObeta-11">[10]</a></sup>&nbsp;An aging star, it has expanded to around 50 times the Sun&#39;s diameter and shines with 660 times its luminosity. It has a faint magnitude 14&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Red_dwarf" title="Red dwarf">red dwarf</a>&nbsp;companion located 29 arcseconds away that takes 76,000 years to complete an orbit.<sup id="cite_ref-kalerbeta_9-1"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-kalerbeta-9">[8]</a></sup>&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Altarf" title="Altarf">Altarf</a>&nbsp;represents a part of Cancer&#39;s body.</span></p> <p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size:9px;">At magnitude 3.9 is&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Delta_Cancri" title="Delta Cancri">Delta Cancri</a>, also known as Asellus Australis.<sup id="cite_ref-kalerdelta_12-0"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-kalerdelta-12">[11]</a></sup>&nbsp;Located 131&plusmn;1 light-years from Earth,<sup id="cite_ref-vanLeeuwen2007_10-1"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-vanLeeuwen2007-10">[9]</a></sup>&nbsp;it is an orange-hued giant star that has swollen and cooled off the main sequence to become an orange giant with a radius 11 times and luminosity 53 times that of the Sun.<sup id="cite_ref-kalerdelta_12-1"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-kalerdelta-12">[11]</a></sup>&nbsp;Its common name means &quot;southern donkey&quot;.<sup id="cite_ref-ridpath_1-3"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-ridpath-1">[1]</a></sup>&nbsp;The star also holds a record for the longest name, &quot;Arkushanangarushashutu,&quot; derived from ancient Babylonian language, which translates to &quot;the southeast star in the Crab.&quot; Delta Cancri also makes it easy to find&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/X_Cancri" title="X Cancri">X Cancri</a>, the reddest star in the sky. Known as Asellus Borealis &quot;northern donkey&quot;,&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gamma_Cancri" title="Gamma Cancri">Gamma Cancri</a>&nbsp;is a white-hued A-type subgiant of spectral type A1IV and magnitude 4.67,<sup id="cite_ref-SIMBAD_13-0"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-SIMBAD-13">[12]</a></sup>&nbsp;that is 35 times as luminous as of the Sun.<sup id="cite_ref-Mcdonald_14-0"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-Mcdonald-14">[13]</a></sup>&nbsp;It is located 181 &plusmn; 2 light-years from Earth.<sup id="cite_ref-vanLeeuwen2007_10-2"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-vanLeeuwen2007-10">[9]</a></sup></span></p> <p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size:9px;"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iota_Cancri" title="Iota Cancri">Iota Cancri</a>&nbsp;is a wide double star. The primary is a yellow-hued G-type bright giant star of magnitude 4.0,<sup id="cite_ref-kaleriota_15-0"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-kaleriota-15">[14]</a></sup>&nbsp;located 330 &plusmn; 20 light-years from Earth.<sup id="cite_ref-vanLeeuwen2007_10-3"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-vanLeeuwen2007-10">[9]</a></sup>&nbsp;It spent much of its stellar life as a B-type main sequence star before expanding and cooling to its current state as it spent its core hydrogen. The secondary is a&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A-type_main_sequence_star" title="A-type main sequence star">white main sequence star</a>&nbsp;of spectral type A3V and magnitude 6.57. Despite having different distances when measured by the HIPPARCOS satellite, the two stars share a common proper motion and appear to be a natural binary system.<sup id="cite_ref-kaleriota_15-1"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-kaleriota-15">[14]</a></sup></span></p> <p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size:9px;">Located 181 &plusmn; 2&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Light-years" title="Light-years">light-years</a>&nbsp;from Earth,<sup id="cite_ref-vanLeeuwen2007_10-4"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-vanLeeuwen2007-10">[9]</a></sup>&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alpha_Cancri" title="Alpha Cancri">Alpha Cancri</a>&nbsp;(Acubens) is a multiple star with a primary component an apparent white main sequence star of spectral type A5 and magnitude 4.26. The secondary is of magnitude 12.0 and is visible in small amateur&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Telescopes" title="Telescopes">telescopes</a>. Its common name means &quot;the claw&quot;.<sup id="cite_ref-ridpath_1-4"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-ridpath-1">[1]</a></sup>&nbsp;The primary is actually two very similar white main sequence stars that are 5.3 AU distant from each other and the secondary is two small main sequence stars, most likely red dwarfs, that are 600 AU from the main pair. Hence the system is a quadruple one.<sup id="cite_ref-kaleralpha_16-0"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cancer_(constellation)#cite_note-kaleralpha-16">[15]</a></sup></span></p> <p style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://www.rollingstone.com/movies/movie-features/trailers-ad-astra-martin-scorsese-bob-dylan-netflix-844556/"><img src="./i.imgur.com/T8TNxjG.png" /></a></p> <p style="text-align: justify;"><span style="font-size:9px;">The&nbsp;<b>Circinus Galaxy</b>&nbsp;(<b>ESO 97-G13</b>) is a&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Seyfert_galaxy" title="Seyfert galaxy">Seyfert galaxy</a><sup id="cite_ref-simbad_2-0"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Circinus_Galaxy#cite_note-simbad-2">[2]</a></sup>&nbsp;in the&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Constellation" title="Constellation">constellation</a>&nbsp;of&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Circinus_(constellation)" title="Circinus (constellation)">Circinus</a>. It is located 4 degrees below the&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Galactic_plane" title="Galactic plane">Galactic plane</a>, and, at a distance of 4.0&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Parsec#Megaparsecs_and_gigaparsecs" title="Parsec">Mpc</a>&nbsp;(13&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Light-year#Definitions" title="Light-year">Mly</a>), and is one of the closest galaxies to the&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Milky_Way" title="Milky Way">Milky Way</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-3"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Circinus_Galaxy#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup>&nbsp;The galaxy is undergoing tumultuous changes, as rings of gas are likely being ejected from the galaxy.<sup>[<i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">citation needed</a></i>]</sup>&nbsp;Its outermost ring is 1400 light-years across while the inner ring is 260 light-years across.<sup>[<i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">citation needed</a></i>]</sup>&nbsp;Although the Circinus galaxy can be seen using a small telescope, it was not noticed until 1977<sup id="cite_ref-4"><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Circinus_Galaxy#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup>&nbsp;because it lies close to the plane of the Milky Way and is obscured by galactic dust. The Circinus Galaxy is a Type II&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Seyfert_galaxy" title="Seyfert galaxy">Seyfert galaxy</a>&nbsp;and is one of the closest known&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Active_galaxy" title="Active galaxy">active galaxies</a>&nbsp;to the&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Milky_Way" title="Milky Way">Milky Way</a>, though it is probably slightly farther away than&nbsp;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Centaurus_A" title="Centaurus A">Centaurus A</a>.</span></p> <p style="text-align: center;"><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=QhxPBrxxaqc"><img src="./i.imgur.com/5bIrFRe.png" /></a></p> <p style="text-align: center;">&quot;weeeee.... I aren&#39;t in them!&quot; s<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jack_Kevorkian">he</a><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Keanu_Reeves">he</a>ki<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Euthanasia">ya</a>nu <strong>&cap;</strong> tit<a href="http://www.gofundme.com/tithehe">hehe</a>&nbsp;|| asia y?</p> <p style=”text-align: justify;”><span style=”font-size:9px;”>Circinus Galaxy produced supernova&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SN_1996cr” title=”SN 1996cr (page does not exist)”>SN 1996cr</a>, which was identified over a decade after it exploded. This supernova event was first observed during 2001 as a bright, variable object in a&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chandra_X-ray_Observatory” title=”Chandra X-ray Observatory”>Chandra X-ray Observatory</a>&nbsp;image, but it was not confirmed as a supernova until years later.</span></p> <p style=”text-align: justify;”><span style=”font-size:9px;”>The Circinus Galaxy is one of twelve large galaxies in the &quot;Council of Giants&quot; surrounding the&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Local_Group” title=”Local Group”>Local Group</a>&nbsp;in the&nbsp;<a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Local_Sheet” title=”Local Sheet”>Local Sheet</a>.<sup id=”cite_ref-10.1093/mnras/stu199_5-0”><a href=”http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Circinus_Galaxy#cite_note-10.1093/mnras/stu199-5”>[5]</a></sup></span></p> <p style=”text-align: center;”><span style=”font-size:14px;”><sup>I ask you, have I ever be || en</sup></span></p> <p style=”text-align: center;”><span style=”color:#FFFFFF;”><span style=”font-size:14px;”><sup>enqueue, enlil and enki – are I on the museum facade or inside wax</sup></span></span></p> <p style=”text-align: center;”><span style=”color:#FFFFFF;”><span style=”font-size:14px;”><sup>phil owe crates and boxes missing from my glyphs truly, GT godspeed.</sup></span></span></p> <p style=”text-align: justify;”>&nbsp;</p> These follow up emails were sent to a smaller audience. /></div></div><div><br /></div><div>Lauren… and girls named Joey … mmmm …</div><div><div><img src=”./i.imgur.com/LhIZcUO.png” width=”288” /><br /></div></div><div><br /></div></div><p><b>Corrado John &quot;Junior&quot; Soprano Jr.</b>, played by <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FDominic_Chianese” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Dominic Chianese</a>,<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJunior_Soprano%23cite_note-NoStonemason-1” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[1]</a> is a <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FFictional_character” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>fictional character</a> from the <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FHBO” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>HBO</a> TV series <i><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Sopranos” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>The Sopranos</a></i>. Usually referred to as &quot;<b>Junior</b>&quot; or &quot;<b>Uncle Jun’</b>&quot;, he is the official boss of the <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FDiMeo_crime_family” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>DiMeo crime family</a> for most of the series. A younger Corrado sometimes appears in <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FFlashback_(narrative)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>flashbacks</a> and is played by <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FRocco_Sisto” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Rocco Sisto</a>. Junior is smart, old-fashioned, stubborn and insecure about his power. Although Junior is portrayed as bitter and deceitful in season one, he shows a more considerate and humorous side of him in the later seasons and reveals a more sensitive side during his illness and house arrest. According to series creator <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FDavid_Chase” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>David Chase</a> the name Junior was taken from one of his own older cousins.</p><div><div dir=”ltr”><h2>Contents</h2></div><ul><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJunior_Soprano%23Background” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>1Background</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJunior_Soprano%23Plot_details” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>2Plot details</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJunior_Soprano%23References” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>3References</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJunior_Soprano%23External_links” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>4External links</a></li></ul></div><h2>Background[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DJunior_Soprano%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D1” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h2><p>In season one it is stated that Junior is 70 years old, placing his birth date in 1928 or 1929. Corrado Soprano, Jr. is the son of Corrado and Mariangela D’Agostino Soprano, Italian immigrants who came over from the town of <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FAriano” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Ariano</a> in 1911.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJunior_Soprano%23cite_note-NoStonemason-1” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[1]</a> Junior is <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FTony_Soprano” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Tony Soprano</a>’s uncle: Junior’s younger brother is Tony’s father <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FList_of_characters_from_The_Sopranos_-_friends_and_family%23John_Francis_%2522Johnny_Boy%2522_Soprano” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Johnny Soprano</a>. He tells the court-ordered psychologist when feigning mental incompetence that he was getting a haircut when he heard about the <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FAssassination_of_John_F._Kennedy” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Assassination of John F. Kennedy</a>. He likes eating Santa Barbara Co. olives from <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSanta_Barbara%2C_California” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Santa Barbara, California</a> and is seen eating them in several scenes. He tells Tony that he admired <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJohn_F._Kennedy” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>John F. Kennedy</a> but did not like his brother <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FRobert_Kennedy” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Robert Kennedy</a> because of Kennedy’s prosecution of <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJimmy_Hoffa” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Jimmy Hoffa</a> and investigation into the <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FInternational_Brotherhood_of_Teamsters” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>International Brot</a>HECRAZY HGC MERCURIAHHHHADAMHELP</p><p><br /></p><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><p><b>What does the “-im” suffix mean at the end of a biblical name?</b></p><p>It indicates the plural form. Cherub<i>im </i>and seraph<i>im </i>are plurals of cherub and seraph, respectively.</p><p>I guess you are thinking about the most used <i>im</i> (ים) word in the Bible, and that would be <i>elohim</i> (אֱלֹהִים), which means gods (again, plural). The interesting thing about this word is that it is used as if it were a singular noun. This means the Hebrew Bible is grammatically incorrect. Deliberately so!</p><p>I am not an expert in ancient languages, and I would not mind being corrected. But, like many other ancient Hebrew words, elohim is based in the Canaanite language discovered at Ugarit. The supreme god of Ugarit was El. (This god is in the Bible too.) And eloh (god) and elohim (gods) seem to be derivatives of this Canaanite god.</p><p>Another consideration is that, when they wrote their Bible, the Jews made a conscious decision to make Judaism a monotheistic faith. The Jews had been worshiping several gods and goddesses since their inception a few hundred years earlier, so this was a major shift. Long-held stories involving several gods had to be adapted into the monotheistic framework. The gods of creation and the the great flood and the tower of Babel now became one god. It is my contention that the reason for the singular elohim and the occasional plural rendition of the god of the Bible is a result of such adaptations.</p></div></div><div><div>529 views · <a target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>4m ago</a></div></div></div></div><div><div><div><div><p>Elohim is something like “Allah” where you might see “all” and think plural. I think of it like a superposition of a “collective consciousness” which is a fairly popular “New Age” idea of what God actually is.</p><p>Not so new.</p><p>Of course, being “Him” I think “singular … and why aren’t you thanking me yet?”</p><p><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fsuez.fromthemachine.org%2FSERENADE.html%3F7B6A7062DA5E5B74” rel=”nofollow” target=”_blank”>SERENADE - </a><a href=”http://suez.fromthemachine” rel=”nofollow” target=”_blank”>http://suez.fromthemachine</a>.org/SERENADE.html for an introduction to my amalgamation of Allah and Elohim, “Allol.” There’s more here, on the connection between Isaac, Ishmael and “Ha” here at <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fthor.lamc.la%2F” rel=”nofollow” target=”_blank”>Adam Mar - THOR - shall Dobrin</a></p></div></div></div></div><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><div><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.quora.com%2FWhat-does-the-im-suffix-mean-at-the-end-of-a-biblical-name%23” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”><div><div><div></div></div><div>Reply</div></div></a></div></div><div></div></div><div></div><div><div><div><div><div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><h1>Semaphore (programming)</h1><div><div>From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div><div></div><div></div><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23mw-head” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Jump to navigation</a><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23p-search” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Jump to search</a><div dir=”ltr”><div><p>In <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FComputer_science” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>computer science</a>, a <b>semaphore</b> is a <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FVariable_(programming)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>variable</a> or <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FAbstract_data_type” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>abstract data type</a> used to control access to a common resource by multiple <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FProcess_(computing)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>processes</a> in a <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FConcurrent_computing” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>concurrent</a> system such as a <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FComputer_multitasking” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>multitasking</a> operating system. A semaphore is simply a variable. This variable is used to solve critical section problems and to achieve process synchronization in the multi processing environment. A trivial semaphore is a plain variable that is changed (for example, incremented or decremented, or toggled) depending on programmer-defined conditions.</p><p>A useful way to think of a semaphore as used in the real-world system is as a record of how many units of a particular resource are available, coupled with operations to adjust that record <i>safely</i> (i.e. to avoid <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FRace_condition” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>race conditions</a>) as units are required or become free, and, if necessary, wait until a unit of the resource becomes available.</p><p>Semaphores are a useful tool in the prevention of race conditions; however, their use is by no means a guarantee that a program is free from these problems. Semaphores which allow an arbitrary resource count are called <b>counting semaphores</b>, while semaphores which are restricted to the values 0 and 1 (or locked/unlocked, unavailable/available) are called <b>binary semaphores</b> and are used to implement <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FLock_(computer_science)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>locks</a>.</p><p>The semaphore concept was invented by <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FDutch_people” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Dutch</a> <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FComputer_scientist” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>computer scientist</a> <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FEdsger_Dijkstra” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Edsger Dijkstra</a> in 1962 or 1963,<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23cite_note-ReferenceA-1” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[1]</a> when Dijkstra and his team were developing an <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FOperating_system” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>operating system</a> for the <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FElectrologica_X8” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Electrologica X8</a>. That system eventually became known as <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FTHE_multiprogramming_system” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>THE multiprogramming system</a>.</p><div><div dir=”ltr”><h2>Contents</h2></div><ul><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23Library_analogy” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>1Library analogy</a><ul><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23Important_observations” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>1.1Important observations</a></li></ul></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23Semantics_and_implementation” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>2Semantics and implementation</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23Examples” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>3Examples</a><ul><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23Trivial_example” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>3.1Trivial example</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23Login_queue” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>3.2Login queue</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23Producer%25E2%2580%2593consumer_problem” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>3.3Producer–consumer problem</a></li></ul></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23Operation_names” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>4Operation names</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23Semaphores_vs._mutexes” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>5Semaphores vs. mutexes</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23See_also” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>6See also</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23References” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>7References</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23External_links” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>8External links</a></li></ul></div><h2>Library analogy[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DSemaphore_(programming)%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D1” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h2><p>Suppose a library has 10 identical study rooms, to be used by one student at a time. Students must request a room from the front desk if they wish to use a study room. If no rooms are free, students wait at the desk until someone relinquishes a room. When a student has finished using a room, the student must return to the desk and indicate that one room has become free.</p><p>In the simplest implementation, the clerk at the front desk knows only the number of free rooms available, which they only know correctly if all of the students actually use their room while they’ve signed up for them and return them when they’re done. When a student requests a room, the clerk decreases this number. When a student releases a room, the clerk increases this number. The room can be used for as long as desired, and so it is not possible to book rooms ahead of time.</p><p>In this scenario the front desk count-holder represents a counting semaphore, the rooms are the resource, and the students represent processes/threads. The value of the semaphore in this scenario is initially 10, with all rooms empty. When a student requests a room, they are granted access, and the value of the semaphore is changed to 9. After the next student comes, it drops to 8, then 7 and so on. If someone requests a room and the current value of the semaphore is 0,<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23cite_note-2” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[2]</a> they are forced to wait until a room is freed (when the count is increased from 0). If one of the rooms was released, but there are several students waiting, then any method can be used to select the one who will occupy the room (like <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FFIFO_(computing_and_electronics)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>FIFO</a> or flipping a coin). And of course, a student needs to inform the clerk about releasing their room only after really leaving it, otherwise, there can be an awkward situation when such student is in the process of leaving the room (they are packing their textbooks, etc.) and another student enters the room before they leave it.</p><h3>Important observations[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DSemaphore_(programming)%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D2” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h3><p>When used to control access to a <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FPool_(computer_science)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>pool</a> of resources, a semaphore tracks only <i>how many</i> resources are free; it does not keep track of <i>which</i> of the resources are free. Some other mechanism (possibly involving more semaphores) may be required to select a particular free resource.</p><p>The paradigm is especially powerful because the semaphore count may serve as a useful trigger for a number of different actions. The librarian above may turn the lights off in the study hall when there are no students remaining, or may place a sign that says the rooms are very busy when most of the rooms are occupied.</p><p>The success of the protocol requires applications to follow it correctly. Fairness and safety are likely to be compromised (which practically means a program may behave slowly, act erratically, <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FHang_(computing)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>hang</a> or <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FCrash_(computing)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>crash</a>) if even a single process acts incorrectly. This includes:</p><ul><li>requesting a resource and forgetting to release it;</li><li>releasing a resource that was never requested;</li><li>holding a resource for a long time without needing it;</li><li>using a resource without requesting it first (or after releasing it).</li></ul><p>Even if all processes follow these rules, <i>multi-resource <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FDeadlock” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>deadlock</a></i> may still occur when there are different resources managed by different semaphores and when processes need to use more than one resource at a time, as illustrated by the <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FDining_philosophers_problem” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>dining philosophers problem</a>.</p><h2>Semantics and implementation[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DSemaphore_(programming)%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D3” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h2><p>Counting semaphores are equipped with two operations, historically denoted as P and V (see <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSemaphore_(programming)%23Operation_names” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>§ Operation names</a> for alternative names). Operation V <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FIncrement_operator” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>increments</a> the semaphore <i>S</i>, and operation P <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FDecrement_operator” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>decrements</a> it.</p><p>The value of the semaphore <i>S</i> is the number of units of the resource that are currently available. The P operation <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FBusy_waiting” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>wastes time</a> or <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSleep_(system_call)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>sleeps</a> until a resource protected by the semaphore becomes available, at which time the resource is immediately claimed. The V operation is the inverse: it makes a resource available again after the process has finished using it. One important property of semaphore <i>S</i> is that its value cannot be changed except by using the V and P operations.</p><p>A simple way to understand wait (P) and signal (V) operations is:</p><ul><li>wait: Decrements the value of semaphore variable by 1. If the new value of the semaphore variable is negative, the process executing wait is blocked (i.e., added to the semaphore’s queue). Otherwise, the process continues execution, having used a unit of the resource.</li><li>signal: Increments the value of semaphore variable by 1. After the increment, if the pre-increment value was negative (meaning there are processes waiting for a resource), it transfers a blocked process from the semaphore’s waiting queue to the ready queue.</li></ul><p>Many operating systems provide efficient semaphore primitives that unblock a waiting process when the semaphore is incremented. This means that processes do not waste time checking the semaphore value unnecessarily.</p><p>The counting semaphore concept can be extended with the ability to claim or return more than one &quot;unit&quot; from the semaphore, a technique implemented in <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FUnix” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Unix</a>. The modified V and P operations are as follows, using square brackets to indicate <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FAtomic_operation” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>atomic operations</a>, i.e., operations which appear indivisible from the perspective of other processes:</p><b>function</b> V(semaphore S, integer I): [S ← S + I] <b>function</b> P(semaphore S, integer I): <b>repeat:</b> [<b>if</b> S ≥ I:

← S − I

<b>break</b>] <p>However, the remainder of this section refers to semaphores with unary V and P operations, unless otherwise specified.</p><p>To avoid <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FResource_starvation” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>starvation</a>, a semaphore has an associated <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FQueue_(data_structure)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>queue</a> of processes (usually with <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FFIFO_(computing_and_electronics)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>FIFO</a> semantics). If a process performs a P operation on a semaphore that has the value zero, the process is added to the semaphore’s queue and its execution is suspended. When another process increments the semaphore by performing a V operation, and there are processes on the queue, one of them is removed from the queue and resumes execution. When processes have different priorities the queue may be ordered by priority, so that the highest priority process is taken from the queue first.</p><p>If the implementation does not ensure atomicity of the increment, decrement and comparison operations, then there is a risk of increments or decrements being forgotten, or of the semaphore value becoming negative. Atomicity may be achieved by using a machine instruction that is able to <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FRead-modify-write” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>read, modify and write</a> the semaphore in a single operation. In the absence of such a hardware instruction, an atomic operation may be synthesized through the use of a <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FMutual_exclusion%23Software_solutions” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>software mutual exclusion algorithm</a>. On <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FUniprocessor” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>uniprocessor</a> systems, atomic operations can be ensured by temporarily suspending <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FPreemption_(computing)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>preemption</a> or disabling hardware <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FInterrupt” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>interrupts</a>. This approach does not work on multiprocessor systems where it is possible for two programs sharing a semaphore to run on different processors at the same time. To solve this problem in a multiprocessor system a locking variable can be used to control access to the semaphore. The locking variable is manipulated using a <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FTest-and-set” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>test-and-set-lock</a> command.</p></div></div></div><blockquote><div><div dir=”ltr”><div><h1>FORMICA QUICKEN?</h1><h1><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fbemessiah.files.wordpress.com%2F2017%2F09%2F6c679-image-746413.png” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”><img src=”http://bemessiah.files.wordpress.com/2017/09/6c679-image-746413.png?w=300” width=”480” /></a></h1><h1>I <i>used to</i> really like wired, before all this happened. Not just the quality and content of their articles, but I also enjoyed the strangely touchable material their covers were often made of. <em>It</em> gave them an extra sort of allure, the “feeling” of a superior product. Today they pointed out that I probably need a computer to give my own writing that same kind of touch-feeling presence that everyone was hoping Jesus would bring; and while statistically that might make some sense… it makes me like the staff writers there just a pinch less; spill over, I’m sure from the barrage of emails that you might consider the E-mail Flood of Noah-ah, that has been not just ignored but <em>shunned</em> by the mass media even to this day… when it’s beyond clear that these are the answers to the questions of the ages and religions and even more pertinent than that, the answers to our problems.</h1><div><div><div><p></p></div></div><div></div><div><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fhadragonbreath.blogspot.com%2F2017%2F09%2Fjust-blame-snake-thats-metaphor-for_43.html” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”></a><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3D1umEXpGHc0E” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”><img src=”http://bemessiah.files.wordpress.com/2017/09/d63c4-image-748212.png?w=300” width=”594” /></a></div><div><br /></div><div></div><div><div><p>Now a days my pleasure reading has declined, along with my pleasure television watching–even in this time when you might consider these things a “job duty,” you know, if I was being paid at all for what I do still believe is some of the most important work that’s ever been done. At the same time I’ve noticed a tangible decline in the number of people commenting on anything I post on Facebook and LinkedIn–two of the places that have stood the test of time and <em>not really</em> banned or blocked this content. Of course, under the hood both have “secret sauce” algorithms to tell you what you should be interested in and on top of that a number of times I’ve noticed that Facebook (and even “don’t be evil” Google) have marked this content as evil-phishing malware and emblazoned them with warnings akin to “<em>only the penitent man may enter</em>“–making click-thru’s that much less frequent. I thought in my head that this lack of conversation was “abnormal” behavior that I linked to the mind control conspiracy that I was very much enthralled with since the early days of my writing. I suppose it is that, it is the product of “Medusa” though as the years have flown by the rank of years; it is becoming more clear that there is a “reason” behind all of this more than subtle control, more than doublethink and sleight of mind. </p><div>September 11, 2017 <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fbemessiah.wordpress.com%2F2017%2F09%2F11%2Fformica-quicken%2F” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”></a><a href=”http://bemessiah.wordpress” rel=”nofollow” target=”_blank”>http://bemessiah.wordpress</a>.com/2017/09/11/formica-quicken/</div></div></div></div><p><br /></p></div></div></div></blockquote><h1>The Freshmen (song)</h1><div><div>From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div><div></div><div></div><a rel=”nofollow”>Brian Vander Ark</a></td></tr><tr><th><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FRecord_producer” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Producer(s)</a></th><td>Donnie Brown (original)<br /><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJerry_Harrison” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Jerry Harrison</a> (album)<br /><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJack_Joseph_Puig” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Jack Joseph Puig</a> (single)</td></tr><tr><th><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Verve_Pipe” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>The Verve Pipe</a> singles chronology</th></tr><tr><td><table><tbody><tr><td>&quot;Cup of Tea&quot; <br />(1997)</td><td>&quot;<b>The Freshmen</b>&quot; <br />(1997)</td><td>&quot;Villains&quot; <br />(1997)</td></tr></tbody></table></td></tr></tbody></table><p>&quot;<b>The Freshmen</b>&quot; is a song by the American alternative rock group <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Verve_Pipe” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>The Verve Pipe</a>. First recorded in 1992, the song was later re-recorded and became the band’s breakthrough hit in early 1997. It is the group’s highest charting single to date.</p><div><div dir=”ltr”><h2>Contents</h2></div><ul><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23Background_and_content” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>1Background and content</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23Versions” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>2Versions</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23Charts_and_certifications” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>3Charts and certifications</a><ul><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23Weekly_charts” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>3.1Weekly charts</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23Year-end_charts” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>3.2Year-end charts</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23Certifications” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>3.3Certifications</a></li></ul></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23Cover_versions” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>4Cover versions</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23See_also” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>5See also</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23References” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>6References</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23External_links” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>7External links</a></li></ul></div><h2>Background and content[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DThe_Freshmen_(song)%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D1” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h2><p>According to the FAQ on &quot;Verve Pipings&quot;, the guitarist and lead singer <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FBrian_Vander_Ark” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Brian Vander Ark</a> wrote the song in 1991 about the guilt he felt from his ex-girlfriend committing <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSuicide” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>suicide</a>.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23cite_note-Verve_Pipeings_FAQ-1” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[1]</a> However, according to an external interview site, Vander Ark said that the suicide was a poetic license; the real incident which inspired the song was when his pregnant girlfriend had an abortion.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23cite_note-2” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[2]</a></p><p>In a 2019 interview with Songfacts, Vander Ark said:</p><blockquote><p>&quot;…It’s for the most part a made-up story, which most of my songs are. These are stories that I come up with, and I do characters. Part of the story was true in the fact that I had gone out with a girl and my buddy had gone out with her after I went out with her, and then I went out with her again and then she ended up getting pregnant and having an abortion. But from there, there’s poetic license that happens and makes the story more dramatic. A neophyte writer that I was, I ended up having her commit suicide, and that never happened.&quot;<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23cite_note-3” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[3]</a></p></blockquote><p>Vander Ark also stated that he never found out whether the baby was his or his friend’s.</p><h2>Versions[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DThe_Freshmen_(song)%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D2” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h2><p>The song first appeared, in acoustic style, on their 1992 album <i><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FI%2527ve_Suffered_a_Head_Injury” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>I’ve Suffered a Head Injury</a></i>. It was recorded a second time and released on the band’s 1996 album, <i><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FVillains_(The_Verve_Pipe_album)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Villains</a></i>. Later that year, the band recorded the song again, this time with the producer <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJack_Joseph_Puig” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Jack Joseph Puig</a>,<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23cite_note-4” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[4]</a> for release as a single on January 27, 1997.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23cite_note-5” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[5]</a> Subsequent pressings of <i>Villains</i> replaced the original album version with the single version. &quot;The Freshmen&quot; peaked at number 5 in the <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FUnited_States” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>United States</a>.</p><p>In addition, a slightly modified single version was released to radio, with Vander Ark singing the final lyrics of the second verse (&quot;thinks about her now and how he never really wept&quot;) in the same melodic sequence as he sings the homologous lyrics at the end of the first verse (&quot;stop a baby’s breath…&quot;), as opposed to his higher-pitched, almost yelled rendering of these lyrics in the version that appeared on the album.</p><h2>Charts and certifications[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DThe_Freshmen_(song)%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D3” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h2><div><table><tbody><tr><td><h3>Weekly charts[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DThe_Freshmen_(song)%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D7” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h2><ul><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FMustard_Plug” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Mustard Plug</a> performed this song for a Michigan radio station. It does not appear on any of their albums.</li><li>In 2004, <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSkott_Freedman” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Skott Freedman</a> released a piano version of the song on his album <i>Judge a Book</i>.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23cite_note-16” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[16]</a></li><li>In 2005, the then-<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FBoston_Red_Sox” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Boston Red Sox</a> pitcher <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FBronson_Arroyo” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Bronson Arroyo</a> covered the song on his first covers album, <i><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FCovering_the_Bases” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Covering the Bases</a></i>.</li><li>In 2010, <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJay_Brannan” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Jay Brannan</a> released a soft indie version of the song as a single, &quot;The Freshmen&quot;.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_Freshmen_(song)%23cite_note-17” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[17]</a></li></ul><h2>See also[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DThe_Freshmen_(song)%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D8” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h2><ul><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=Js1qF9v5y3wKTeE7wVgw&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FNumber_one_modern_rock_hits_of_1997” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Number one modern rock hits of 1997</a></li></ul><div>Lyrics</div><div><div><div><div>When I was young I knew everything<br />And she a punk who rarely ever took advice<br />Now I’m In later Scandinavian folklore, the ambiguity surrounding the entities gives way to negative portrayals.</p><p><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=1JtpwxBRacXEXg5iqCT3&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2Fhashtag%2Fcouzh%3Fsource%3Dfeed_text%26epa%3DHASHTAG” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>#COUZH</a></p><p><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=1JtpwxBRacXEXg5iqCT3&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Ffromthemachine.org%2FCURSOR.html” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”><img src=”./i.imgur.com/JDkobK0.png” width=”653” /></a><br /></p><p>fam..<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=1JtpwxBRacXEXg5iqCT3&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fplaylist%3Flist%3DPLgYKDBgxsoMNdwAiaHhYCBefI0d0Iqs0V” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>.. &quot;ous</a>&quot;<br /></p><p>Æsir – &quot;Ansuz&quot; redirects here. For the runic character, see Ansuz (rune).</p><p>In Old Norse, ǫ́ss (or áss, ás, plural æsir; feminine ásynja, plural ásynjur) is a member of the principal pantheon in Norse religion. This pantheon includes Odin, Frigg, Thor, Baldr and Týr.[1] The second pantheon is known as the Vanir. In Norse mythology, the two pantheons wage war against each other, which results in a unified pantheon.</p><p>The cognate term in Old English is ōs (plural ēse) denoting a deity in Anglo-Saxon paganism. The Old High German is ans, plural ensî.[2] The Gothic language had ans- (based only on Jordanes who glossed anses with uncertain meaning, possibly ‘demi-god’ and presumably a Latinized form of actual plural *anseis).[3] The reconstructed Proto-Germanic form is *ansuz (plural *ansiwiz). The ansuz rune, ᚫ, was named after the Æsir.</p><p>My special word ‘ASSIM&quot; which dissects as &quot;as sim&quot; is a corruoption of the singular Norse for &quot;God&quot; and the Hebrew pluralization &quot;IM&quot; you can see here in YELADIM, which I read as something like &quot;it’s multiple.&quot;</p><p><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=1JtpwxBRacXEXg5iqCT3&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fl.facebook.com%2Fl.php%3Fu%3Dhttp%253A%252F%252Fjel.jewish-languages.org%252Fwords%252F611%253Ffbclid%253DIwAR3mgvXhumuMzp1WtFQ7e0863KMf6xm5CPQL-uaxzkDkfp9WZnlJtm1G188%26h%3DAT3eoMAxDwa2nPdTAWlRmBrrB5a9fnd-W8q4ZqF3X-rgMCUsTIsj2lCVdAXKtZmkOyGmMMYeOatj_N3L2pYEA_nEeFMEn8XmhU96-cP2YYiTdKlaD2VOzYKnGV4HvHxWQr4bPNltYSNpS9D76t1kGa6JO55v9fWc6GPNyWzuog” rel=”nofollow” target=”_blank”></a><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=1JtpwxBRacXEXg5iqCT3&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fjel.jewish-languages%2F” rel=”nofollow” target=”_blank”>http://jel.jewish-languages</a>.org/words/611 <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=1JtpwxBRacXEXg5iqCT3&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2Fhashtag%2Fyeladim%3Fsource%3Dfeed_text%26epa%3DHASHTAG” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>#yeladim</a> - &quot;students / children&quot;</p><p>The “im” is a suffix used in the Hebrew tongue that makes a singular noun a plural noun. For example, the Hebrew word for prophet is Navi’ and the Hebrew word for “prophets,” in the plural, is Navi’im. in a place so far from here there is no path in timespace from here to there… on a planet called Cherrynoble, and before that Kyshtym, and before that Mayak; savress named Backiam was born into a world that had been laid desolate by nuclear holocaust, by toxic waste, and by an invasion of ants the size of pickles. The remnant of their people lived in a few small camps that are about as close to our cities as anything else in their world, though there was nothing to buy or sell, no toys, no computers, and no cars. They worked each and every day in laboratories with only one goal in mind, to build a machine to travel back in time and reverse the cataclysm that had destroyed their once flourishing civilization.<br /><br />Progress was made, and first terminals were built that allowed the past to be viewed like a television show; a team called Pastwatch was created in order to search for the most opportune possible moment to change their past, avert the series of disasters that had befallen them, and to build a better future. While they prepared, a virtual world was built as a sort of Ark to carry all the living souls that remained alive back into the past, so that they could live again in this new world. A singular point was never decided upon, but rather a transitional period that began with few changes in the distant past, and then much more frequent and bigger changes as they approached the time of the cataclysm. <br /><br />So as not to make any mistakes or errors, and perhaps as the biggest error of all–or the saving grace of everything that is; the Pastwatch group decided to run a simulation in their virtual time machine to ensure that they were successful. It was not days, but years that went by as they prepared to &quot;make the leap home.&quot;<br /><br />In that very first year, the machines scoured through the history of everything and made a virtual copy of each and every soul, and imported into the machines memory.<br /><br />In the second year, a message was written down, an explanation of what had happened to their world, and a plea to change the practices that had created the problems that destroyed the world. This message was delivered to the virtual world signed &quot;Everything that Ever Was&quot; and presented as a scroll nailed to the inside of the front door of each and every home. <br />Much to the surprise of Pastwatch, each and every single message was taken down and thrown away, nobody had even read a single word.<br /><br />On the third day of Creation, this same messages was coded and hidden within a book, and along with that book a number of historical events were slightly modified; direct changes to the memories of those that had experienced them so that these events would serve as waypoints on the path to change. <br /><br />On the fourth day, the names of each and every person were changed to protect the innocent, and the coded message continued; now being hidden in the names of the changed events and the people who witnessed them. In every name, another sentence, another clue to seeing not just the waypoints but the entire map of what had happened and advice on how to make it better.<br /><br />In the final hour of that fourth day, a reckless young programmer queried the machine to answer how many of the events were solved and how many of the people involved had successfully transitioned from the virtual reality to the much more advanced world that Cherrynoble had created for themselves. The young man asked for a result with such a high certainty, that the machine had no choice but to run a full simulation; each and every consciousness inside the machine was active and sentient; and the machine wrote a message on the skies above the world whose name had changed to Earth. With only minutes left, a number of possible welcome messages were debated… I mean, were run through a secondary simulation by the machine; and with only seconds remaining, this is what the entire world saw:<br /><br /><br /><strong>Hi, I’m Adam. Here we are. </strong><br /><br />For your second J, connect these points: 1) this very moment in time to 2) the Hanging Gardens of Babylon to Adam of Eden, and 3) the city Ur to the words &quot;you are&quot; and the questions that drives us…<br /><br /> &quot;<strong>what is the beginning of Civilization?</strong>&quot; and &quot;<strong>Y</strong>?&quot;<br /></p><p><br /></p><p><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=1JtpwxBRacXEXg5iqCT3&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fqz.com%2Fquartzy%2F1460772%2Fthe-meaning-of-excelsior-the-latin-word-marvel-legend-stan-lee-made-his-motto%2F” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”><img src=”./i.imgur.com/L4yniPM.png” width=”543” /></a><br /></p><p>&quot;an no tat ion&quot; anno <i><b>notayshun</b></i>!</p></div></div></div>^</div><div>&quot;cztar&quot;</div><div><div><table border=”0” cellpadding=”8” cellspacing=”0”><tbody><tr><td><a href=”http://geotrack.email/?utm_source=gmail&amp;utm_medium=signature&amp;utm_campaign=viralSignature” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”><img src=”http://s3-us-west-2.amazonaws.com/geotrackcdn/icon32.png” width=”24” /></a></td><td>Sender notified with <a href=”http://geotrack.email/?utm_source=gmail&amp;utm_medium=signature&amp;utm_campaign=viralSignature” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>GeoTrack</a></td></tr></tbody></table></div></div><img src=”http://pxl-mailtracker.com/pixel/P3cabPr8EVPxs9ToxNTd?rid=P3cabPr8EVPxs9ToxNTd” width=”1” /></div> </div><img src=”http://pxl-mailtracker.com/pixel/0FcMuMqiU06csOIt61D0?rid=0FcMuMqiU06csOIt61D0” width=”1” /><img width=”0” src=”http://geotrack.email/ext/1JtpwxBRacXEXg5iqCT3.png?gtk=YWRhbUBmcm9tdGhlbWFjaGluZS5vcmc%3D” /></div> </div> </div> <hr/> <link rel=”icon” type=”image/x-icon” href=”/favicon.ico”> <link rel=”stylesheet” type=”text/css” href=”/css/view.css”> <link href=”http://fonts.googleapis.com/css?family=Martel:300,400|Open+Sans:300,400,600|Roboto+Slab:300,400” rel=”stylesheet”> <meta name=”viewport” content=”width=device-width, initial-scale=1”> <link rel=”canonical” href=”http://www.publishthis.email/running-with-paper,-hands-….-and-opinions-things-we-lost-in-the-fire.-意見手紙-iken-te-shi-y-HksefFARV”> </head> <body onscroll=”scroll()”> <div class=”page-margin page” dir=”ltr”> <h1>Running with Paper, Hands …. and Opinions – &quot;things we lost in the fire.&quot; 意見手紙 iken-te-shi / yìjiàn shǒu zhǐ</h1>

<div class=”body”><div dir=”ltr”><div><div>As a brief commentary, I’m not sure how many people would instantly respond to the name of Janet’s band … with exactly what I did–with a &quot;lit&quot; and &quot;linked&quot; connection to the game Paper, Rock and Scissors–it’s almost impossible to believe and be sure that this connection is part of the original intent of naming tjheir band &quot;Running with Scissors&quot; … or realize perhaps that the &quot;missing Rock&quot; in our &quot;head&quot; another <i><font face=”comic sans ms, sans-serif”>unintentionally </font><font face=”times new roman, serif”>or perhaps near perfect reference to Zeus and the idea that the Mine</font><font face=”arial black, sans-serif”>rvan</font><font face=”times new roman, serif”> core of his mind is .. quite literally the world we see around us here. Minerva, encased within the mind of God.</font></i></div><div><br /></div>Rock; paper, opinion… <i>shoot?!</i></div><div><i><br /></i></div><div>I’m sharing this today because this song literally re-ignited my … somewhat waning and nearly lost belief that there are still people here who want to see &quot;opinions&quot; (and even, perhaps &quot;hands&quot; return to the process of ascension that I’d all but given up on ever returning to see &quot;heroes&quot; or &quot;heroine&quot; or &quot;avenues&quot; connecting Heaven and Hell’s Kitchen. </div><div><br /></div><div>I know, you should look around you and see a significant … somewhat strange &quot;doublehollering&quot; of assistance and echoes and additions and … what have you to the message that is … an outline of a legend of an overlay to the Map that connects our Atlas to the Matrix to … well, to these roads to futures once-or-more-taken and yet to me completely hidden. It’s that though, that they’re hidden completely to me, these futures, and &quot;Indian Pines&quot; and … and nearly any kind of direct comment or addition other than,</div><div><br /></div><div>&quot;We hear you, Adam.&quot; I even have a friend on Facebook named &quot;Adam Speaks&quot; as if we need to be reminded. I wonder if that person comes from a time where speaking is rare, and if you find that thought or possibility, that a &quot;Last Supper&quot; did away not just with hunger or our need for &quot;23 complete amino acid chains&quot; but also with conversation …. </div><div><br /></div><div>… scary?</div><div><br /><div dir=”ltr”><div><div><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.youtube.com%2Fwatch%3Fv%3DqYl4_-1OMFA” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”><img src=”./i.imgur.com/LD6QQb3.png” /></a><br in to long</div><div><br /></div><div>’Cause there’s no &quot;I&quot;</div><div>No <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fpetrovical.reallyhim.com%2F” Factor</a></i> in 2011 where she finished in fifth place.</p><p>Devlin’s debut album was launched in October 2012 via <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23Music_videos” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>5.5Music videos</a></li></ul></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23Tours” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>6Tours</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23References” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>7References</a></li><li><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23External_links” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>8External links</a></li></ul></div><h2>Early life and education[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DJanet_Devlin%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D1%26editintro%3DTemplate%3ABLP_editintro” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h2><p>Devlin is the youngest of four children to Aquinas and Pat Devlin and has three elder brothers: Jason, Gavin and Aaron. Prior to entering <i>The X Factor</i>, she lived with her parents and brothers in Gortin, County Tyrone, Northern Ireland. She attended an <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FIrish_medium_education” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Irish language</a> <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FPre-school” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>pre-school</a>,<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23cite_note-NosMag-4” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[4]</a> and later attended <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FDrumragh_Integrated_College” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Drumragh Integrated College</a> where she completed her GCSE’s.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23cite_note-5” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[5]</a></p><p><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FCourtney_Love” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Courtney Love</a> has stated in interviews that she believes Janet and her family to be distant relatives of <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FKurt_Cobain” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Kurt Cobain</a>,<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23cite_note-6” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[6]</a> though Devlin has stated that she is unaware of any connection. Devlin’s only performing experience before auditioning for <i>The X Factor</i> was singing in her school, pubs and local talent shows. She had uploaded a number of videos of her singing to her official channel on <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FYouTube” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>YouTube</a>.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23cite_note-7” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[7]</a></p><h2>Career[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DJanet_Devlin%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D2%26editintro%3DTemplate%3ABLP_editintro” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h2><h3>2011: <i>The X Factor</i>[<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fw%2Findex.php%3Ftitle%3DJanet_Devlin%26action%3Dedit%26section%3D3%26editintro%3DTemplate%3ABLP_editintro” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>edit</a>]</h3><p>In 2011, Devlin auditioned for the eighth series of <i><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FThe_X_Factor_(UK_series_8)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>The X Factor</a></i>.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23cite_note-8” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[8]</a> Her audition was screened on 20 August 2011, where she performed <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FElton_John” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Elton John</a>’s &quot;<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FYour_Song” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Your Song</a>&quot;.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23cite_note-youtube1-9” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[9]</a> Her audition was successful as all four judges, <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FLouis_Walsh” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Louis Walsh</a>, <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FTulisa” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Tulisa</a>, <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FKelly_Rowland” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Kelly Rowland</a> and <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FGary_Barlow” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Gary Barlow</a>, put her through to the next round. She performed <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FColdplay” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Coldplay</a>’s &quot;<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FFix_You” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Fix You</a>&quot; in week 1 of the live shows and was put through to the next round by mentor <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FKelly_Rowland” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Kelly Rowland</a>, as there was no public vote in the first week. Devlin topped the public vote more times than any other act, receiving the most public votes for the first four weeks of voting (weeks 2, 3, 4 and 5)<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23cite_note-10” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[10]</a><a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23cite_note-11” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[11]</a> and reached the quarter-final before ending up in the bottom two with <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FMisha_B” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Misha B</a>. She was voted off by Walsh and Tulisa with Rowland refusing to vote. However voting statistics revealed that Devlin received more votes than Misha B meaning if the result went to deadlock, Devlin would’ve advanced to the semi-final and Misha B would’ve been eliminated. Devlin’s song in the sing off was &quot;<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FChasing_Cars” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Chasing Cars</a>&quot;. During the live shows, <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FCourtney_Love” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Courtney Love</a> tweeted <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FSimon_Cowell” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Simon Cowell</a> to offer to give Devlin one of <a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FNirvana_(band)” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>Nirvana</a>’s tracks for the show.<a href=”http://geotrack.email/ext/l?idx=R6D7Iwq9RPOgLg96wyrD&amp;ret=http%3A%2F%2Fen.wikipedia.org%2Fwiki%2FJanet_Devlin%23cite_note-12” target=”_blank” rel=”nofollow”>[12]</a> This, however, did not transpire.</p><h4><i>The X Factor</i> Performances[<a
